# pagedump
Script to dump page table entries for two processes to know the sharing proportions. 

===============How to run========================
```
python pagedump.py <pid1> <pid2>
```

===============Sample o/p========================
```
Process Summary for PID 1586

Swap                :0       Kb
USS                 :0       Kb
Shared              :0       Kb

SwapBacked          :624     Kb
```
